06/11/2024, 14:29 - Gulnaz Mam: *Space on Wheels - Space exhibition at Ivy Estate, Wagholi on Nov 6, 2024* 

Time : 9am to 5pm

A collaboration between ISRO and Vibha, is a mobile science exhibition designed to bring space education to students and the public across India. It features interactive displays of space missions, hands-on STEM learning, and models of rockets and satellites. Targeted especially at rural and underserved areas, this initiative inspires young minds and fosters inclusivity in science education. By bringing space exploration directly to communities, "Space on Wheels" promotes awareness of India's achievements and empowers future scientists and engineers.

This exhibition in Wagholi is brought to you by Ivy Estate Federation, Ivy Apartment and Villas, Heartfulness and Vibha team. It is supported by participating educational institutions - SNBP Wagholi, JSMP University, SRCOE College and Raisoni College

08/11/2024, 11:48 - Naru: <!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <title>Simple Form</title>
</head>
<body>
    <form action="hello" method="post">
        Name: <input type="text" name="name"><br>
        <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    </form>
</body>
</html>
import javax.servlet.ServletException;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServlet;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.io.PrintWriter;

public class HelloServlet extends HttpServlet {
    protected void doPost(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) throws ServletException, IOException {
        String name = request.getParameter("name");
        response.setContentType("text/html");
        PrintWriter out = response.getWriter();
        out.println("<html><body>");
        out.println("Hello, " + name + "!");
        out.println("</body></html>");
    }
}

08/11/2024, 12:46 - Abh√Æ: *Cookies Program*
import java.io.IOException;
import javax.servlet.ServletException;
import javax.servlet.http.Cookie;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServlet;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;

public class CookieServlet extends HttpServlet {
    protected void doGet(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response)
            throws ServletException, IOException {

        response.setContentType("text/html");
        
        // Retrieve the 'username' cookie if it exists
        Cookie[] cookies = request.getCookies();
        String username = null;

        if (cookies != null) {
            for (Cookie cookie : cookies) {
                if ("username".equals(cookie.getName())) {
                    username = cookie.getValue();
                    break;
                }
            }
        }

        response.getWriter().println("<html><body>");
        
        if (username == null) {
            // If no username cookie found, display form to enter the username
            response.getWriter().println("<h2>Enter your name</h2>");
            response.getWriter().println("<form method='POST'>");
            response.getWriter().println("Name: <input type='text' name='username' required>");
            response.getWriter().println("<input type='submit' value='Submit'>");
            response.getWriter().println("</form>");
        } else {
            // If username cookie is found, greet the user
            response.getWriter().println("<h2>Hello, " + username + "!</h2>");
        }
        
        response.getWriter().println("</body></html>");
    }

    protected void doPost(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response)
            throws ServletException, IOException {
        
        // Get the username from the form input
        String username = request.getParameter("username");
        
        if (username != null && !username.isEmpty()) {
            // Create a cookie to store the username
            Cookie userCookie = new Cookie("username", username);
            userCookie.setMaxAge(86400); // Set the cookie to last for 1 day
            response.addCookie(userCookie);
        }
        
        // Redirect back to the same servlet to display the greeting
        response.sendRedirect("CookieServlet");
    }
}

17/03/2025, 12:19 - Deep Deshmukh...: def encrypt(text, s):
    result = ""  # Initialize the result string
    
    # Traverse through each character in the text
    for i in range(len(text)):
        char = text[i]
        
        # Encrypt uppercase characters
        if char.isupper():
            result += chr((ord(char) + s - 65) % 26 + 65)
        
        # Encrypt lowercase characters
        elif char.islower():
            result += chr((ord(char) + s - 97) % 26 + 97)
        else:
            result += char  # Non-alphabetical characters are added as-is
    
    return result

# Test the function
text = "ATTACKATONCE"
s = 4
print("Text : " + text)
print("Shift : " + str(s))
print("Cipher: " + encrypt(text, s))

import android.os.Bundle;
import android.widget.TextView;
import android.widget.TimePicker;

import androidx.activity.EdgeToEdge;
import androidx.appcompat.app.AppCompatActivity;
import androidx.core.graphics.Insets;
import androidx.core.view.ViewCompat;
import androidx.core.view.WindowInsetsCompat;

public class MainActivity extends AppCompatActivity {
    TimePicker timePicker;

    TextView textView;

    @Override
    protected void onCreate(Bundle savedInstanceState) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState);
        setContentView(R.layout.activity_main);
        textView = findViewById(R.id.tv);
        timePicker = findViewById(R.id.tp);
        timePicker.setOnTimeChangedListener(new TimePicker.OnTimeChangedListener() {
            @Override
            public void onTimeChanged(TimePicker view, int hourOfDay, int minute) {
                String time = String.format("%02d:%02d", hourOfDay,  minute);
                textView.setText("Selected Time:" + time);


            }


        });
    }
}
